   if ( window.ue && window.ue.tag ) {
        window.ue.tag('dpi_' + Math.round(window.devicePixelRatio), window.ue.main_scope);

  <script type="text/javascript">
   var bopCSM = {
          csmAvailable: typeof window.uet === 'function',
          pageType: 'home',
          setCSMProp:   function (method, prop, key) {
            if (this.csmAvailable) {
                window[method](prop, key, {wb:1});
            }
          },
          fireAjaxMarker: function(marker, scope){
              if(this.csmAvailable){
                  window.uet( marker, scope );
                  window.ues( "ctb", scope, "1" );
                  window.uex( "ld", scope );
              }
          },
          fireMarker:  function (marker) {
              if(this.csmAvailable) {
                  window.uet(marker);
              }
          },
          fireMarkers: function (markers) {
              for(var i = 0; i < markers.length; i++){
                  this.fireMarker(markers[i]);
              }
          },
          checkCacheElementsByMarker: function(container, marker){
              var elements = container.getElementsByClassName(marker);

              if(elements.length > 0){
                  for (var i = 0;i < elements.length; i++) {
                      if(!elements[i].complete){
                          return;
                      }
                  }
                  bopCSM.fireMarker(marker);
              }
          },
          allElementsLoadedFromCache: function(){
              var container = document.getElementById('siteContainer');
              if(container != null) {
                  bopCSM.checkCacheElementsByMarker(container, 'af');
                  bopCSM.checkCacheElementsByMarker(container, 'cf');
              }
          } ,
          fireImageCompleteWidgetTag: function(currentCount, maxCount, csmWidgetName){
              if(currentCount === maxCount){
                  this.setCSMProp('uex', 'ld', csmWidgetName);
              }
          },
          allImagesLoaded: function(elementId, querySelector, csmWidgetName ){
              var i,
                  images,
                  imageCounter = 0,
                  imageLength = 0,
                  imageContainer = document.getElementById(elementId);

              if (!imageContainer || !this.csmAvailable) {
                return;
              }

              images = imageContainer.querySelectorAll(querySelector);
              imageLength = images.length;

              for (i = 0; i < imageLength; i++){

                if(images[i].complete){
                  imageCounter++;
                  this.fireImageCompleteWidgetTag(imageCounter, imageLength, csmWidgetName);
                } else {
                  var imageOnLoad =images[i].onload;
                  images[i].onload = function(){
                      imageCounter++;
                      bopCSM.fireImageCompleteWidgetTag(imageCounter, imageLength, csmWidgetName);
                      if(typeof imageOnLoad === 'function'){
                          imageOnLoad.apply(this, arguments);
                      }
                  }
                }
            }
          },
    };
    //Ensure every page gets at least the af and cf events
    //if other components emit these later those will take precedence
    bopCSM.fireMarker('af');
    bopCSM.fireMarker('cf');

    //Adding this function for backwards compatability, so that we can push out without breaking the page.
    function setCSMProp(method, prop, key) {
        bopCSM.setCSMProp(method, prop, key);
    }

    function csmAllImagesLoaded(elementId, querySelector, csmWidgetName){
        bopCSM.allImagesLoaded(elementId, querySelector, csmWidgetName);
    }
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   window.addEventListener(
        "DOMContentLoaded",
        function() {

            if (window.performance &&
                window.performance.timing &&
                window.performance.timing.domContentLoadedEventStart &&
                window.performance.timing.navigationStart) {
                const clickToContentInteractive = window.performance.timing.domContentLoadedEventStart - window.performance.timing.navigationStart;
                digitalData.v2.page.attributes.performance.clickToContentInteractive = clickToContentInteractive;
            }
        });

                            #search-container.desktop #search-suggestion-container {

        <form action="/products" data-ajax="false" enctype="application/x-www-form-urlencoded" id="search-form" method="get" name="searchForm">
         <div class="search-input-container">
          <span data-search-img="search-icon" id="search-icon">
          </span>
          <input autocapitalize="none" autocomplete="off" autocorrect="off" class="search-input" data-search-field="search-input" id="search-input" maxlength="50" name="query" placeholder="Search" spellcheck="false" type="text"/>
          <span class="search-clear" data-search-btn="clear" id="search-clear">
           Clear
          </span>
          <input id="search-suggestion-used" name="searchSuggestion" type="hidden" value="false"/>
         </div>
        </form>
        <div class="search-results-container" id="search-suggestion-container">
         <input id="search-suggestion-search-site-param" type="hidden" value="WOMENS"/>
         <input id="search-suggestion-locale-param" type="hidden" value="en_US"/>
         <input id="search-suggestion-site-id-param" type="hidden" value="1000"/>
         <input id="max-results-param" type="hidden" value="10"/>
         <div id="search-arrow">
         </div>
         <div id="search-suggestions">
          <section class="search-suggestion-section" id="text-search-section">
           <ul class="text-search-suggestions" id="text-search-suggestions">
           </ul>
          </section>
         </div>
        </div>
        <script type="text/javascript">
         document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
                                "use strict";
                                var queuedRequestExecution = null,
                                        textSuggestionCache = {},
                                        cacheSizeLimit = 20,
                                        visibleClass = "visible",
                                        activeClass = "active",
                                        currentSuggestion = -1,
                                        upArrow = 38,
                                        downArrow = 40,
                                        utilityElements = {
                                            shopElement: document.getElementsByClassName('shop-other')[0],
                                            locationElement: document.getElementsByClassName('nested-location-list')[0],
                                            languageElement: document.getElementsByClassName('nested-language-list')[0],
                                            currencyElement: document.getElementsByClassName('nested-currency-list')[0],
                                            logoElement: document.getElementsByClassName('logo')[0],
                                            cartElement: document.getElementById("shopping-cart-link")
                                        },
                                        searchForm = {
                                            formElement: document.getElementById("search-form"),
                                            searchSiteParameterElement: document.getElementById("search-suggestion-search-site-param"),
                                            localeParameterElement: document.getElementById("search-suggestion-locale-param"),
                                            maxResultsElement: document.getElementById("max-results-param"),
                                            //TODO: consolidate this param with search site
                                            siteIdElement: document.getElementById("search-suggestion-site-id-param"),

                                            searchContainerElement: document.getElementById("search-container"),
                                            searchTextInputElement: document.getElementById("search-input"),
                                            searchSuggestionContainerElement: document.getElementById("search-suggestion-container"),
                                            textSearchSectionElement: document.getElementById("text-search-section"),
                                            textSearchSuggestionContainerElement: document.getElementById("text-search-suggestions"),
                                            //param passed to website used to indicate whether a suggestion was used. We may want to search for an alternative.
                                            searchSuggestionUsedElement: document.getElementById("search-suggestion-used"),
                                            searchClearBtnElement: document.getElementById("search-clear"),
                                            searchIcon: document.getElementById("search-icon"),
                                            searchArrowElement: document.getElementById("search-arrow"),
                                            searchViewAllElements: document.getElementsByClassName("search-view-all"),
                                            searchSuggestionClass: "search-suggestion",
                                            desktopClass: "desktop",
                                            mdotClass: "m-dot",

                                            // Close Btn interaction will be moved out of portlet code. Needed for short term test
                                            searchCloseBtnElement: document.getElementById("top-nav-search-close")
                                        },
                                        // Get the api URL base
                                        getApiRoot = function() {
                                            // API root URL is embedded in the page
                                            var apiRootElem = document.getElementById("api-root");
                                            if (apiRootElem !== undefined && apiRootElem.dataset.href) {
                                                return apiRootElem.dataset.href;
                                            } else {
                                                throw new Error("No API root is configured");
                                            }
                                        },
                                        // Call to get the search suggestions
                                        executeSearchSuggestion = function(baseUrl, params, selector, cache) {
                                            var xmlHttpRequest = new XMLHttpRequest();
                                            var url = baseUrl + "?lang=" + encodeURIComponent(params.locale) +
                                                    "&siteId=" + encodeURIComponent(params.siteId) +
                                                    "&limit=" + encodeURIComponent(params.maxResults) +
                                                    "&includeProducts=false" +
                                                    "&q=" + encodeURIComponent(params.searchText);

                                            xmlHttpRequest.onreadystatechange = function () {
                                                if (xmlHttpRequest.readyState === XMLHttpRequest.DONE) {
                                                    if (xmlHttpRequest.status === 200) {
                                                        // if the contents of the search box have changed since this request was made, don't show the suggestions; the change will have triggered another request
                                                        if (searchForm.searchTextInputElement.value === params.searchText) {
                                                            var responseText = xmlHttpRequest.responseText;
                                                            replaceSearchSuggestion(selector, responseText);

                                                            if (Object.keys(cache).length < cacheSizeLimit) {
                                                                cache[params.searchText] = responseText;
                                                            }
                                                            updateSuggestionElements();
                                                        }
                                                    }
                                                }
                                            };

                                            xmlHttpRequest.open("GET", url);
                                            xmlHttpRequest.setRequestHeader ("Accept", "application/json");
                                            xmlHttpRequest.send();
                                        },
                                        // suggestionElementSelector will be set with suggestionText
                                        replaceSearchSuggestion = function(suggestionElementSelector, suggestionText) {
                                            var suggestionElement = document.querySelector(suggestionElementSelector);
                                            var suggestionParentElement = suggestionElement.parentNode;
                                            var fragment = _parseSuggestionJsonToElement(suggestionText);
                                            suggestionParentElement.replaceChild(fragment, suggestionElement);
                                        },
                                        _parseSuggestionJsonToElement = function(json) {
                                            // Get Get a list to build into
                                            var container = document.createElement("ul");
                                            container.setAttribute("id", "text-search-suggestions");
                                            container.setAttribute("data-suggestions-info", "container");

                                            var responseObject = JSON.parse(json);
                                            for (var i = 0; i < responseObject.searchSuggestions.length; i++) {
                                                for (var j = 0; j < responseObject.searchSuggestions[i].searchSuggestions.length; j++) {
                                                    // Build the element
                                                    var suggestion = document.createElement("li");
                                                    suggestion.textContent = responseObject.searchSuggestions[i].searchSuggestions[j].suggestion;
                                                    suggestion.setAttribute("class", "search-suggestion");
                                                    suggestion.setAttribute("data-suggestions-info", "suggestion");

                                                    // Add it to the container list
                                                    container.appendChild(suggestion);
                                                }
                                            }

                                            return container;
                                        },
                                        // State changed - update suggestions
                                        updateSuggestionElements = function() {
                                            // Search Suggestions
                                            if (document.getElementsByClassName(searchForm.searchSuggestionClass).length > 0) {
                                                searchForm.textSearchSectionElement.classList.add(activeClass);
                                            } else {
                                                searchForm.textSearchSectionElement.classList.remove(activeClass);
                                                searchForm.textSearchSectionElement.classList.remove(visibleClass);
                                            }

                                            searchSuggestionContainerDisplay();
                                        },

                                        // State changed - determine search container display
                                        searchSuggestionContainerDisplay = function () {
                                            // Hide the search results container if there is nothing to display
                                            if (searchForm.textSearchSectionElement.classList.contains(activeClass) &&
                                                    searchForm.searchTextInputElement.value.length > 1) {
                                                searchForm.searchSuggestionContainerElement.classList.add(visibleClass);
                                            } else {
                                                searchForm.searchSuggestionContainerElement.classList.remove(visibleClass);
                                            }
                                        },
                                        activateClear = function() {
                                            if (searchForm.searchContainerElement.classList.contains(searchForm.mdotClass)) {
                                                searchForm.searchClearBtnElement.classList.add(activeClass);
                                            }
                                        },
                                        activateSearch = function() {
                                            searchForm.searchContainerElement.classList.add(activeClass);
                                            searchSuggestionContainerDisplay();

                                            setTimeout(function() { searchForm.searchTextInputElement.focus(); }, 10);

                                            window.addEventListener('click', inactivateSearchModalEventHandler);
                                        },
                                        inactivateSearchModalEventHandler = function(event) {
                                            if (searchForm.searchContainerElement.classList.contains(searchForm.desktopClass) &&
                                                    !searchForm.searchContainerElement.contains(event.target)) {
                                                // Clicked outside the Search Modal
                                                searchForm.searchContainerElement.classList.remove(activeClass);
                                                searchForm.searchSuggestionContainerElement.classList.remove(visibleClass);
                                            }
                                        },
                                        inactivateClear = function() {
                                            searchForm.searchTextInputElement.value = "";

                                            searchForm.textSearchSectionElement.classList.remove(activeClass);
                                            searchForm.searchClearBtnElement.classList.remove(activeClass);

                                            searchForm.searchTextInputElement.focus();
                                        };

                                searchForm.formElement.addEventListener("click", activateSearch);
                                searchForm.searchClearBtnElement.addEventListener("click", inactivateClear);


                                if (searchForm.searchContainerElement.classList.contains(searchForm.mdotClass)) {
                                    // We get a focus event for Mobile when invoked from Nav.  Need to invoke activateSearch if not currently active.
                                    searchForm.searchTextInputElement.addEventListener("focus", function(event) {
                                        if (searchForm.searchTextInputElement.value === "") {
                                            inactivateClear();
                                            activateSearch();
                                        }
                                    });
                                }


                                for (var i = 0; i < searchForm.searchViewAllElements.length; i++) {
                                    searchForm.searchViewAllElements[i].addEventListener("click", function(event) {
                                        searchForm.formElement.submit();
                                    });
                                }

                                searchForm.formElement.addEventListener("submit", function(event) {

                                    if (!searchForm.searchTextInputElement.value || !searchForm.searchTextInputElement.value.trim()) {
                                        event.preventDefault();
                                        event.stopPropagation();
                                    } else if (currentSuggestion !== -1) {
                                        var suggestions = document.getElementsByClassName("search-suggestion");
                                        if (!suggestions || suggestions.length === 0) {
                                            return;
                                        }
                                        var target = suggestions[currentSuggestion];
                                        searchWithSuggestion(target);
                                    } else {
                                    trackEventWithArguments("Search Executed", {searchTerm: searchForm.searchTextInputElement.value});
                                    }
                                });

                                // Tracks clicking search suggestion text and submits with that value
                                searchForm.searchSuggestionContainerElement.addEventListener("click", function(event) {
                                    var target = event.target;
                                    searchWithSuggestion(target);
                                });

                                searchForm.searchIcon.addEventListener("click", function(event) {
                                    trackEvent("Search Open Click");
                                    if (hasMinimumSearchTextForSubmit()) {
                                        searchForm.formElement.submit();
                                    }
                                });

                                // Tracks the user clicks with the Search box
                                searchForm.searchTextInputElement.addEventListener("click", function(event) {
                                    trackEvent("Search Open Click");
                                });

                                function trackEvent(eventName) {
                                    if (typeof _satellite !== 'undefined' && typeof _satellite.track === 'function') {
                                      _satellite.track(eventName);
                                    } else {
                                      console.error("_satellite didn't exist or didn't have a track method for event " + eventName);
                                    }
                                  }

                                function trackEventWithArguments(eventName, jsonData) {
                                    if (typeof _satellite !== 'undefined' && typeof _satellite.track === 'function') {
                                      _satellite.track(eventName, jsonData);
                                    } else {
                                      console.error("_satellite didn't exist or didn't have a track method for event " + eventName);
                                    }
                                }

                                function searchWithSuggestion(target) {
                                    if (target.classList.contains(searchForm.searchSuggestionClass)) {
                                        searchForm.searchTextInputElement.value = target.textContent;
                                        trackEventWithArguments("Search Executed", {searchTerm: searchForm.searchTextInputElement.value});
                                        // Setting place holder to empty since it is not being replaced in m-dot.
                                        searchForm.searchTextInputElement.placeholder = "";
                                        searchForm.searchSuggestionUsedElement.value = "true";

                                        // Hide the Search Suggestions Container since the form is being submitted
                                        searchForm.searchSuggestionContainerElement.classList.remove(visibleClass);

                                        searchForm.formElement.submit();
                                    }
                                }

                                searchForm.searchTextInputElement.addEventListener("keydown", function(event) {
                                    // If there are no search suggestions do not check which key was pressed
                                    if (!searchForm.textSearchSectionElement.classList.contains(activeClass)) {
                                        return;
                                    }
                                    if (event.keyCode === upArrow) {
                                        event.preventDefault();
                                        moveThroughSuggestionList(-1);
                                    } else if (event.keyCode === downArrow) {
                                        event.preventDefault();
                                        moveThroughSuggestionList(1);
                                    }
                                }, true);

                                function moveThroughSuggestionList(offset) {
                                    var suggestions = document.getElementsByClassName("search-suggestion");
                                    if (!suggestions || suggestions.length === 0) {
                                        return;
                                    }
                                    var node = suggestions[currentSuggestion];
                                    if(node){
                                        node.classList.remove("selected-suggestion");
                                    }
                                    var numberOfSuggestions = suggestions.length;
                                    currentSuggestion += offset;
                                    if (currentSuggestion < 0) {
                                        currentSuggestion = 0;
                                    } else if (currentSuggestion >= numberOfSuggestions) {
                                        currentSuggestion = numberOfSuggestions-1;
                                    }
                                    //Make call to change highlighted suggestion here
                                    node = suggestions[currentSuggestion];
                                    node.classList.add("selected-suggestion");
                                }

                                function hasMinimumSearchTextForSubmit() {
                                    var hasMinimumSearchText = false;
                                    var minimumTextInputSizeForSuggestions = 1;
                                    if (searchForm.searchTextInputElement.value && searchForm.searchTextInputElement.value.length >= minimumTextInputSizeForSuggestions) {
                                        hasMinimumSearchText = true;
                                    }

                                    return hasMinimumSearchText;
                                }

                                function hasMinimumSearchTextForSuggestions() {
                                    var hasMinimumSearchText = false;
                                    var minimumTextInputSizeForSuggestions = 2;
                                    if (searchForm.searchTextInputElement.value && searchForm.searchTextInputElement.value.length >= minimumTextInputSizeForSuggestions) {
                                        hasMinimumSearchText = true;
                                    }

                                    return hasMinimumSearchText;
                                }

                                searchForm.searchTextInputElement.addEventListener("keyup", function(event) {
                                    //continuing with the existing queuing pattern to a) avoid extra requests and b) avoid flickers that would otherwise happen when typing rapidly

                                    if (event.keyCode === upArrow || event.keyCode === downArrow) {
                                        return;
                                    }
                                    if (queuedRequestExecution) {
                                        clearTimeout(queuedRequestExecution);
                                    }

                                    if (searchForm.searchTextInputElement.value && searchForm.searchTextInputElement.value.length > 0) {
                                        activateClear();
                                    } else {
                                        inactivateClear();
                                    }

                                    if (!hasMinimumSearchTextForSuggestions()) {
                                        // Clear out search suggestions since they will be stale.  We only invoke suggestion when more then 2 characters are present.
                                        document.getElementById("text-search-suggestions").innerHTML = "";
                                        searchForm.textSearchSectionElement.classList.remove(activeClass);

                                        updateSuggestionElements();
                                    }

                                    queuedRequestExecution = setTimeout(function() {
                                        //get searchSite and locale from params on-page
                                        var params = {
                                            searchSite: searchForm.searchSiteParameterElement.value,
                                            locale: searchForm.localeParameterElement.value,
                                            searchText: searchForm.searchTextInputElement.value,
                                            siteId: searchForm.siteIdElement.value,
                                            maxResults: searchForm.maxResultsElement.value
                                        };

                                        if (params.searchText && params.searchText.length > 1) {

                                            // Handle Text Suggestion
                                            if (textSuggestionCache[params.searchText]) {
                                                var responseText = textSuggestionCache[params.searchText];
                                                replaceSearchSuggestion("#text-search-suggestions", responseText);

                                                updateSuggestionElements();
                                            } else {
                                                executeSearchSuggestion(getApiRoot() + "/search/suggestion", params, "#text-search-suggestions", textSuggestionCache);
                                            }

                                        } else {
                                            updateSuggestionElements();
                                        }
                                        queuedRequestExecution = null;
                                    }, 100);

                                });

                                // Tracks the user clicks with the Cross Site Link
                                utilityElements.shopElement.addEventListener("click", function(event) {
                                    trackEvent("Cross Site Click");
                                });

                                // Tracks the user clicks with Location
                                utilityElements.locationElement.addEventListener("click", function(event) {
                                    trackEvent("Location Click");
                                });

                                // Tracks the user clicks with Language
                                utilityElements.languageElement.addEventListener("click", function(event) {
                                    trackEvent("Language Click");
                                });

                                // Tracks the user clicks with Currency
                                utilityElements.currencyElement.addEventListener("click", function(event) {
                                    trackEvent("Currency Click");
                                });

                                // Tracks the user clicks with Cart Icon
                                utilityElements.cartElement.addEventListener("click", function(event) {
                                    trackEvent("Cart Icon Click");
                                });

                                // Tracks the user clicks with Logo
                                utilityElements.logoElement.addEventListener("click", function(event) {
                                    trackEvent("Logo Click");
                                });
                            });
        </script>
       </div>
      </li>
     </ul>
    </div>
   </div>
  </div>

  </div>

  </script>

    <script>
     ;(function() {
        const elements = document.getElementById("Container-PCL2T8L").getElementsByClassName("csmEnabled");
        for(let i=0; i < elements.length; ++i) {
            let hasCSMFired = false;
            elements.item(i).addEventListener("load",function(e) {
                if(window.uet && !hasCSMFired){
                     window.uet('af'); window.uet('cf');
